The Jin army is unwilling for the Feng troops to enter Shanxi, and the Feng troops are also very suspicious of the Jin army, so the Jin and Feng troops are disarming each other. The Central Army will prepare to cross the river to pursue [the Feng troops] after the northern bank of the Yellow River, north of Bian[liang] and Zhengzhou, has been completely suppressed. The Central Army advancing to the west captured Luoyang on the 9th, and the vanguard, Yang Hucheng’s army, has passed through Xin'an, Mianchi, and Shaanzhou and is advancing towards Tongguan. The remnants of the Feng army have retreated and gathered in Tongguan. Now I am in charge of political affairs, but because the commissioners of the various committees have not all arrived, the date of taking office has not been decided yet.”

Current Provincial Affairs: At noon on the 15th, [the reporters’ group] visited Acting Chairman of the Provincial Government Zhang Fang at the Provincial Government but did not find him. Li Jingliu, who is acting for the Director of Civil Affairs, received the [reporters’ group] and said regarding the current state of provincial affairs: “The Henan Provincial Committee left the province in its entirety at the same time as the Han Fuju army was ordered to withdraw eastward. After that, Yan Xueshan was appointed chairman, and after Wan Xuancai, [who was also] appointed chairman, was captured, Li Xiaolan was appointed acting chairman. The situation had already fallen into disarray. Zhang Fang, who was both the commissioner of the Henan Provincial Committee and the director of the Construction Department, was summoned by telegram from Chiang [Kai-shek] and organized a temporary provincial government in Guide on June 1. At that time, the original provincial committee consisted of only Zhang Fang and Zhang Honglie. So Zhang Fang acted as chairman and Zhang Honglie acted as director of the secretariat, which was divided into three sections: Wang Hongxian was director of general affairs, Wang Youmei was director of finance, and Li Jingliu was director of political affairs. At that time, only forty or so of Henan Province’s one hundred and ten-odd counties were under [the provincial government’s] control. Afterwards, Zhang Fang was trapped in Haozhou for more than forty days, and the provincial administration became even more difficult. After Zhang Fang escaped, Chiang appointed him as the Commander-in-Chief of the Twentieth Route Army and ordered him to collect the miscellaneous troops of Henan Province. Because of this, Zhang Fang again left Guide for the Shahe River, staying in Yancheng for more than a month and collecting the troops of Song Tiancai, Zhao Guanying, and Jiao Wendian, gathering them in western Henan to await orders. After Kaifeng was recovered, Zhang Fang arrived in Kaifeng from the west, and the temporary provincial government also moved from Guide to Kaifeng on the 5th. However, the original provincial committee consisted of only Zhang Fang and Zhang Honglie, which was difficult to distribute [among provincial] affairs. It was decided that Zhang would act as chairman and concurrently as director of the Construction Department and the Finance Department, and Zhang Honglie would concurrently be the director of the Education Department and the Civil Department, while Wang Hongxian would act as director of the Construction Department, Wang Youmei would act as director of the Finance Department, and Li Jingliu would act as director of the Civil Department, separately taking over provincial affairs and starting to reorganize them. However, after the great war, most of the personnel in the political and financial organs of each county were conveniently appointed by military organs, and it was difficult to unify [them] administratively. In particular, it will be difficult to provide relief to the disaster areas because large sums of money are needed. When the temporary provincial government was in Guide, it organized a disaster area investigation and consolation group, and distributed forms to the counties for filling out and reporting. It also appealed to the central government and relief agencies to request aid. After moving to Kaifeng, it requested Commander-in-Chief Chiang to allocate 200,000 yuan for the consolation of war casualties in the war zones. Currently, the central government has approved the allocation of 100,000 yuan to handle emergency relief. However, because the disaster is severe and the funds are small, it is still difficult to distribute [them]. It is currently working on reorganizing the relief association so that it can be responsible for handling the relief efforts in various places, such as Minquan, Lanfeng, Weishi, Ningling, Qi County, Kaocheng, Taikang, Luyi, Zhecheng, Shangqiu, Chenliu, Tongxu, Yuancheng, Weishi, Xinzheng, Lin Ying, Xuchang, and Huaiyang. These are all severely affected areas, with losses in each county mostly exceeding one million. Even with large sums of money for relief during this recent period, it will not be easy to recover. It is the good fortune of the people of Henan that the press is fully publicizing the failure to unify administration and the urgent need for disaster relief.” Later, when the reporter asked about the fact that the Zhang’s replacement as acting chairman had been appointed to the new provincial committee and heard that he had resigned, Li said that Zhang was from Xin'an County and that his family had a Minsheng coal mine in Xin'an. This time, Feng Yuxiang became jealous of him for managing the situation in Henan, and the family mines in Shaanxi and Xin'an were searched and confiscated. Moreover, [Zhang] was imperiled in Haozhou for many days and ran around Yancheng on military affairs. At this point, he also wanted to rest a bit and did not have any other meaning. Zhang is currently resting, so you gentlemen did not find him when you visited. The new provincial committee will be able to take office within the next few days. The provincial government of Henan still needs to conduct a thorough reorganization, but its essentials will not be outside the unification of administration and disaster relief. It is my humble opinion that the Central Plains can be pacified from now on, and the suffering experienced by the people of Henan is nothing short of being suffered on behalf of the people of the entire country. I hope that the people of the country will have a sense of sympathy and provide appropriate relief.”

A Glimpse of Party Affairs: The Henan Provincial Party Headquarters is located in the Iron Pagoda Temple. Due to the hurried journey, there was no time to visit. Li Jingliu, who was originally the secretary-general of the provincial party headquarters, is very familiar with party affairs. According to him, after leaving Kaifeng, the Henan Provincial Party Committee first performed its duties in Zhumadian and then moved to Xinyang. The Kaifeng Provincial Party Headquarters was occupied by the Reorganization Faction. After the recapture of Kaifeng, the Party Headquarters returned to Kaifeng from Xinyang just one or two days ago. However, the committee is not complete. For the time being, Han Lilun, the former standing committee member, is acting as standing committee member, Zhang Shanyu is acting as director of the Propaganda Department, Xue Guanghan is acting as director of the Training Department, and Chen Panling is acting as director of the Organization Department. There are five committee members in total, including Li He. Reorganization of party affairs in the various counties is currently being planned and implemented.

Municipal Construction: Although Kaifeng was in the aftermath of war, the original construction could still be seen. A common people’s village in Kaifeng City was built from the railway station to the city. The entire village is in the shape of a circle, with the Sun Yat-sen Clubhouse in the middle. The buildings are single-story and covered with tiles, simple and sturdy. The entire village is inhabited by common people and vendors, and is well-organized. It is conceivable that a lot of effort was put into the planning when it was first built. The streets in the city are wide and lack stone, so bricks were used as the roadbed. A safety water tank filled with clear water is prepared in front of every shop along the road and sprinkled three times a day, so that even in an area full of sand, there is no flying dust. The famous Dragon Pavilion in the northwest corner of the city has been converted into Sun Yat-sen Park, with a steady stream of orderly visitors. The Xiangguo Temple has been converted into the Sun Yat-sen City Market, where stalls and vendors gather. Inside there is a Revolution Memorial Hall, Art Gallery, Industry Museum, Common People's Rest Room, Common People's Lecture Hall, Folk Music Pavilion, Common People's Park, etc. Next to the Xiangguo Temple is the People's Assembly Hall, with towering walls and three stories, which can accommodate more than 10,000 people. The Bell and Drum Tower has been converted into the Sun Yat-sen Library, with reading rooms for books and newspapers. A workers’ rest room is also located near the provincial government, with provincial notices posted there. After all, it is unavoidable that [the city] has a state where the scale and spirit are still present but has lost its essence since it is in the aftermath of war. After the reporters finished their inspection in Kaifeng, they boarded a military vehicle westward at 7:00 p.m. on the 15th and arrived in Zhengzhou at 11:00 p.m. that evening (16th).

The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department Convenes a Winter Defense Conference

County Magistrates and Others are Selected and Organized into Groups to Attend the Conference

The First Group Meeting Opened Yesterday

In order to prepare for winter defense and rectify police affairs, the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department has convened, and has organized into groups, county magistrates, chiefs of public security bureaus, chiefs of various districts of the Provincial River Police Brigade. Starting from the 20th, they will come to the province for meetings according to the selection sequence. The meeting period for each group is set for a total of three days, with each day's meeting hours being from 8:00 a.m. to 12:00 p.m. in the morning and from 1:00 p.m. to 5:00 p.m. in the afternoon. It is heard that after the meeting ends in the future, the resolutions of each group's meeting will be summarized and reported to the provincial government for record by the Director of the Civil Affairs Department. The dates for the selected county magistrates, chiefs of public security bureaus, and chiefs of various districts of the Provincial River Police Brigade meetings are as follows: First Group: Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Qingpu, Fengxian, Jinshan, Chuansha, Taicang, Jiading, Baoshan, Wuxian, Changshu, Kunshan, Wujiang, Wujin, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, River Police Districts 1, 2, 3: from October 20 to 22, Year 19. Second Group: Jiangning, Jurong, Lishui, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jintan, Liyang, Yangzhong, Jiangdu, Yizheng, Baoying, River Police District 5: from October 28 to 30, Year 19. Third Group: Chongming, Qidong, Haimen, Jingjiang, Nantong, Rugao, Taixing, Huaiyin, Huaian, Funing, Yancheng, Taixian, Dongtai, Xinghua, Gaoyou, River Police Districts 4 and 6: The meeting dates will be notified separately. Fourth Group: Siyang, Lianshui, Tongshan, Fengxian, Lixian, Xiaoxian, Dangshan, Pixian, Suqian, Suining, Donghai, Guanyun, Shuyang, Ganyu: The meeting dates will be notified separately. Yesterday (the 20th) was the opening day of the first group meeting. The meeting was held in the assembly hall of the Provincial Government at 3:00 p.m. The attendees included Civil Affairs Department Secretary Tai Danian, Lin Yichang, Hu Huisheng, Section Chiefs Lu Changgan, Zhao Enju, Zhang Zhongli, Tian Bingzhang, Lin Wenqin, Guan Ji'an, Shanghai County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jinghua, Songjiang County Magistrate Jin Qingzhang, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhu Ying, Nanhui County Magistrate Kong Chong, Public Security Bureau Chief Jin Runzhang, Qingpu County Magistrate Yu Ding, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhu Hua, Fengxian County Magistrate Shen Qing, Public Security Bureau Chief Li Zhibin, Jinshan County Magistrate Lu Quan, Public Security Bureau Chief Shi Pengcheng, Chuansha County Magistrate Tu Guangjun, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhu Shanyuan, Taicang County Magistrate Tao Mu, Public Security Bureau Chief Xi Ziwei, Jiading County Magistrate Chen Chuande, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhu Shou, Baoshan County Magistrate Qiu Mingjiu, Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jing, Wuxian County Magistrate Huang Sichen, Public Security Bureau Chief Zou Jing, Changshu County Magistrate Tan Jigui, Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kun, Kunshan County Magistrate Pang Shusen, Public Security Bureau Chief Qin Jieren, Wujiang County Magistrate Wu Jia, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhou Zhaonan, Wujin County Magistrate Wu Deyao, Public Security Bureau Chief Yin Peng, Yixing County Magistrate Sun Gongxin, Public Security Bureau Chief Wu Yizeng, Wuxi County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia, Public Security Bureau Chief Xu Jigui, Jiangyin County Magistrate Li Leng, Public Security Bureau Chief Li Zonggang, Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Fu, River Police District 1 Chief Chen Jiekun, River Police District 2 Chief Mao Mujun, River Police District 3 Chief Shen Weiying, and Security Section Wang Bojian. First, Chairman Hu Pu'an delivered an opening speech, stating that today's meeting is a type of meeting to plan and rectify public security matters. The provincial government's responsibility is the security of the people of the entire province, and the county government's responsibility is the security of the people of the entire county. Security is relatively easy to manage in the spring, summer, and autumn seasons, but in winter, petty criminals and unscrupulous elements will take the opportunity to cause trouble. Since the Republic of China, due to political reforms, the social security situation in these past few years should be given even more attention than before. We are now discussing winter defense matters, but the period of defense is not only in winter; we must be responsible for defense at all times. However, winter is even more important. There have been quite a few banditry disasters in various counties this year. In the province,

Page 9

Domestic News

The methods of trying to fundamentally eliminate banditry every day cannot be applied in general. The biggest reason is that there is no connection between counties. For example, if there are bandits in County A, County B will take a spectator's attitude. If troops are sent to suppress the bandits, they have already heard the news and fled to another county. If a county government has the strength, it can certainly eliminate [bandits], but the strength of one county is not enough to fundamentally eliminate bandits, so it is necessary for each county to connect together to suppress [the bandits]. This winter defense conference is for everyone to discuss methods of joint defense, research good opinions, increase strength, and start eliminating bandits. This is the most important point of opening the winter defense conference. If each county can earnestly suppress [the bandits] and implement joint defense plans, the bandit disasters in this province will be eliminated soon. Another point is that the situations in each county are different. Some have sufficient self-defense forces, and some do not have enough self-defense forces. If we want to eliminate bandit disasters, we must first rectify ourselves. Therefore, winter defense and rectification of police affairs are the same thing. It is hoped that the many cases submitted by each county will be thoroughly discussed and reasonable solutions will be produced. Once resolutions have been discussed and decided, they must be taken back to each county for sorting out and vigorous implementation, so that the people have the hope of living and working in peace and the county government can be considered to have fulfilled its responsibilities. Following that, Section Chief Zhang Zhongli and Jiangyin County Magistrate Li Leng and others gave speeches. After the speeches, the entire group took a photo. At 4:00 p.m., the meeting opened for discussion. It was decided that a general meeting will be held at 2:00 p.m. today (the 21st).

The Truth About the Longjing Village Incident

Japanese Police Conduct Armed Night Raid

Mistakenly Shot and Killed at a Checkpoint

Harbin Correspondence: Regarding the conflict between the Japanese police and our military and civilians in Longjing Village on the 7th of this month, the Japanese news agency is expanding propaganda. We were unable to obtain the true story due to the distance and difficult roads, so we relied entirely on the Japanese side's fabrication of rumors. Yesterday, we received a very detailed telegram from various public organizations in Longjing Village stating the cause of the incident. The transcription is as follows: "At 9:00 p.m. on the 6th of this month, a Chinese pear vendor surnamed Yang was involved in a quarrel and fight with a Korean man, Yu Jijun, in Funing Alley in Longjing Village, Yanji, because Yu was stealing pears. The Chinese man was seriously injured. At that time, both the Chinese and Korean parties were preparing to go to the Commercial Bureau to reason things out. It happened that a Commercial Bureau police officer intervened to mediate. Suddenly, many Japanese police officers came and wanted to arrest both our Chinese and the police officer together. The Chinese public was aroused to public indignation and gathered to reason with the Japanese police. The Japanese police were furious and fired a shot to intimidate the crowd. At that time, the Japanese police station on Dalu Road heard the gunshot and another five or six Japanese police officers poured out and actually took our police officer away. When the Commercial Bureau heard the news, it immediately dispatched the bureau's translator, along with two police officers, to negotiate. The Japanese police station admitted that it was a misunderstanding and handed over our police officer to the Commercial Bureau's translator to take back. This matter had come to an end. Afterwards, the Japanese police sought trouble for no reason, causing a misunderstanding, which is a separate matter. We fear that rumors will be lost in transmission, so we are sending a special telegram to report it." Another telegram said: "Longjing Village is an important town on the Yanbian border. Because of defense, martial law has been in effect for several months recently. However, at 10:00 p.m. on the 6th of this month, more than a dozen armed men suddenly opened fire on the sentry. In self-defense, the sentry returned fire, killing two of the enemy and wounding one. After investigation, it was learned that the two who were killed were all wearing Japanese police uniforms, one holding a Binyin pistol and the other holding a Type 38 rifle. According to the Chief Inspector of the Japanese Consulate, Secret Tail, the injured person is Takahashi, and those killed are Yoshioka and Fujita, etc. No terms of negotiation have yet been proposed, but 103 armed Japanese police officers were sent from Korea as early as the 9th. They paraded on the same day, causing panic among merchants and civilians. It is heard that they are also planning to successively increase the number of police officers. An investigation shows that more than a dozen armed Japanese police officers are deliberately demonstrating in the dark of night during this period of martial law. It is evident that they intend to cause trouble by freely entering our inland under the pretext of increasing the number of police officers. The Japanese newspaper is therefore making one-sided propaganda. Please correct it immediately. In order to save the country, the merchants, farmers, workers, and students of Yanbian are all so angry that they want to die. We hope that everyone will advocate justice. The Yanbian Federation of Agriculture, Commerce, Industry, and Students in Longjing Village bows and presents [this information]. Truly." The Japanese consul stationed in Jilin has already lodged a strongly worded protest on the 9th of this month. The provincial government has telegraphed Zhang Shuhan, the head of the Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office, to investigate the matter locally and has ordered the garrison commander, Ji Xing, to reply with the truth (13th).

Wuhu Quick Letter

The Anhui Province Sixth District Bandit Suppression Commander is Lv Xueshu, the commander of the Capital Garrison Regiment stationed in Wuhu. Recently, the regiment was ordered to be transferred back to Nanjing, and the Sixth District Bandit Suppression Command was also abolished. Recently, the Anhui Provincial Bandit Suppression Commander-in-Chief, Wei Lihuang, reported that the bandit disasters in southern Anhui have not been suppressed and that large numbers of communist bandits have been discovered in the Langxi and Guangde areas, and that bandit suppression cannot be the responsibility of anyone. He therefore requested and was approved by Commander-in-Chief Jiang to appoint Xu Guoting, the commander of the 341st Regiment of the 57th Division stationed in Wuhu, as the new Sixth District Bandit Suppression Commander yesterday by telegram, and ordered him to organize a command headquarters in Wuhu immediately and be responsible for suppressing the communist bandits in Yiguang and other eleven counties.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau and Xu Guoting's regiment of the 57th Division stationed in Wuhu have reorganized the joint military-police inspection office for the sake of local security. It was established today. In addition to the military and police sending teams to form a joint patrol team, the merchant corps also sent a platoon of soldiers to join. The director of the office is Su Kaiyuan, the adjutant of Xu Guoting, and the deputy director is Sun Wenhua, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau.

Chen Diaoyuan has ordered Ruan Zhaochang's troops, who are now in Liuhe, to station themselves in southern Anhui for training now that the military affairs at the front have come to an end. Ruan's troops are prepared to depart and yesterday specially telegraphed the Wuhu Municipal Public Security Bureau to find housing for the troops to station in.

Yesterday evening, more than a hundred bandits suddenly came to Huangchi Town, 40 miles from Wuhu, and plundered the town. The extent of the losses is unknown. People have now been sent to investigate (20th).

Local Correspondence

松江

The First Purchasing Cooperative Holds Autumn Member Congress: The Songjiang First Purchasing Cooperative is a farmer-organized fertilizer purchasing organization. Since its establishment in May of last year, members have had strong confidence in the cooperative. On the 19th of this month, the third member congress was held, proposing an additional 5,000 yuan in share capital, which was unanimously approved. It is said that the share subscription is extremely enthusiastic.

Various Agencies Unsuccessful in Retaining the Water Police Team: The First Team of the First District of the Water Police Force of Jiangsu Province stationed in Songjiang used to be stationed in Minhang. Now, because Jinshan has repeatedly reported bandit police incidents, local communities have petitioned the province to move the team to Jinshan to deter them. However, the county chamber of commerce, the property disposal office, and the district office of this county believe that Songjiang is a strategic location between Shanghai and Hangzhou, with the westward transportation of willow dregs and the northern reliance on the Nine Peaks. Bandit police incidents are frequently reported in the four townships. Except for the team's location in Songjiang, it is easier to respond to emergencies. Therefore, they telegraphed Chen, the district chief of Minhang, the other day to avoid any changes. Now, they have received a response from District Chief Chen, stating that one team's defense area also covers Songjiang and Jinshan. Recently, due to the weakness of the military force in Jin County, bandits have repeatedly harassed Lvxiang, Yanxia, and Qianxu and other public security sub-bureaus. The defense regiment's firearms were also seized by bandits, and the people were in a state of panic and could not live in peace. Therefore, there was a proposal to move the first division to Jinshan, and it was submitted to the Ministry of Civil Affairs for approval. Your county has a stronger strength and has a customs anti-smuggling team stationed there. In fact, there is relatively little to worry about. Our district has limited resources to meet local needs and has to make slight changes. It is said that the team will have to move in this year.

Organizing a Review and Price Equalization Committee: After the end of the price equalization in this county, it was discovered that there were malpractices in the ninth district, which had to be thoroughly reviewed to restore public funds. The county party headquarters proposed the organization of a review committee at the last party headquarters conversation meeting, which was approved. The price equalization bureau convened a closing meeting today. The review committee members recommended by the county party headquarters were Lu Changlin and Yang Tianduo, and the county government recommended Zhou Qi and Zhang Yinzi. The price equalization committee members recommended Zhang Huanzhi, Lu Kangsheng, and Zhang Shaomei as members. A meeting will be convened on a regular basis.

Qingpu

A Quarrel Leads to a Fatal Case: Ke Yongquan, the shopkeeper of Yongtai Youbinghao in Zhanglianyong Township, Third District of this county, had a quarrel with Shen Youqing and Shen Yumei, the shopkeepers of Yan Yi Mao and Jin Xin Chang Youbinghao in the town. The two Shen brothers, on the other day, carried wooden weapons and rushed to the Yongtai Youbinghao, seeking to beat Ke on the head, causing him to fall to the ground with serious injuries. The shopkeeper reported to the local Public Security Second Sub-bureau, and the bureau only arrested the two murderers the next day and fined them. However, Ke suffered excessive injuries and the treatment was ineffective. He died two days later. The corpse family reported to the county for an autopsy. The county government sent personnel to perform an autopsy and found that Ke had been beaten to death before his death. The county government ordered the corpse family to collect the corpse and wait for the arrest of the murderer for investigation and prosecution.

A Police Officer Sentenced to Imprisonment for Fraud: Ma Yixiang, a police officer of the First Team of the County Police Force, falsely asked for leave last month and sneaked to the home of Shi Yongkui, a prisoner serving a sentence in Tiansheng Village. He falsely claimed to Shi's mother, Shi Wu, that Shi was seriously ill and that if she could pay 150 yuan, he could arrange for him to be released. Shi's mother believed it to be true and went by boat to the city to reluctantly raise the money from relatives and friends and handed it over to the police officer. They went to the county government to wait for the redemption. After Ma entered, he immediately left from the back door and sneaked back to the team. Shi Wu waited for a long time and asked people before she realized she had been cheated. The county government learned of this and ordered the First Team to detain the criminal and bring him to the county for repeated interrogation. The criminal could not deny it and was sentenced to six years and eight months of imprisonment in accordance with the regulations on the abuse of public office to serve as a warning.

Suzhou

Retrial of the Shanghai Murder Case: Fang Jianwen, who lived on the overpass of a toothbrush factory on Huining Road in Shanghai, was killed by his wife, Yu, in collusion with her lover, Zhang Huairen, on the evening of the ninth day of the first month of the lunar calendar last year. Fang's body was abandoned in a nearby cemetery. The murderer immediately fled. On the thirteenth of this month, the body was discovered by a scavenger. The police district in charge reported it and the local court sent personnel to perform an autopsy. Zhang Huairen was arrested immediately and handed over to the local court, which sentenced him to death. Zhang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court, which upheld the original judgment. Zhang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent it back to the High Court for a retrial last month. Yesterday (21st), Lin Dawen, the presiding judge of the First Criminal Division of the High Court, summoned the local security chief Jian Qing and Fang Jianru, the brother of the deceased, to court for a trial.

Large Batch of Military Prisoners Escorted from Shanghai to Suzhou: The Shanghai Garrison Command escorted more than 200 military prisoners to the Suzhou Second Army Prison yesterday (21st). The Public Security Bureau learned of the chaos in advance and dispatched a platoon of police and two platoons of mounted patrolmen to the station to wait. After arriving in Suzhou at 5:00, they cooperated in escorting the prisoners to the Second Army Prison outside Panmen for detention.

Suspected Reactionaries Escorted to the Province for Interrogation: The Public Security Bureau dispatched the investigation team leader Zhou Hongjiang at 12:48 noon yesterday (21st) to escort ten suspected reactionaries, including Yao Xuan and Gu Rongchuan, to the province for interrogation.

Wuxi

Silk Factories Advocate for Government Funding to Maintain Operations: The Wuxi Silk Factory Guild convened an extraordinary general membership meeting yesterday morning regarding the joint Zhejiang-Shanghai petition to the government to allocate funds to maintain operations and issue public bonds. Representatives from 39 factories attended, with Qian Fenghao presiding. He first reported on the case of requesting the government to issue silk industry public bonds to rescue the industry. The method for each factory to independently decide on the public bond loan and the issue of loan responsibility were resolved at the 18th general meeting. However, the method for repaying the debt after the loan is of great importance to the interests of the industry. Because the industry requested a reconsideration, it should be carefully studied and decided so that the five Wuxi representatives can follow it when attending the meeting. After the representatives present made a long and practical discussion, they finally resolved: (1) The loan amount that Wuxi should receive must be received and distributed evenly by the Wuxi company. (2) The establishment of a bank will not be recognized temporarily after the silk industry maintenance funds are borrowed. (3) Shanghai Qiahe and Suzhou Ruifeng are silk factories run by foreign merchants. Since they are open for business in Chinese territory, they should be treated equally. When the silk from these two factories is exported, 20 taels should be deducted to show uniformity. If the above three points cannot be done, the Wuxi silk factories would rather withdraw and not borrow this maintenance fee. The above resolutions were resolved and the five Wuxi representatives recorded the case and carried it to Shanghai to present it for discussion at the special committee meeting for requesting funds today (22nd).

Resolution of the Strike at the Defeng Silk Factory: The workers of the Defeng Silk Factory outside Nanmen went on a full strike on the 17th, organizing a strike committee due to the capital's implementation of the guild's resolution to reduce wages by 20% and cancel the bonus work. After two days of stalemate, the county party rectification committee and the workers' rectification committee, fearing that reactionary elements would incite trouble, specially sent Lu Zhenwen and Liu Qidi to investigate the factory workshop and ordered them to send representatives to negotiate with the factory. The factory's chief manager Che Yang Peifeng, as the full representative, jointly negotiated and decided on the following methods: (1) The labor representative is responsible for notifying all workers to resume work uniformly on the same day. (2) The capital representative is responsible for paying the wages for September in full after the resumption of work, without any deduction. (3) The wages for October will be determined by the county party headquarters, the county government, the workers' rectification committee, and the silk factory guild. The capital shall not unilaterally reduce wages. (4) The salaries of all employees shall be handled in the same way as the workers. The above articles were signed on the spot by the representatives of both labor and capital, and work was resumed on the same day.

The County Director of Liyang Was Arrested and Escorted to the Province: Liyang County suffered repeated disturbances from the Broadsword Society bandits last year, and the local vitality was greatly damaged. Recently, Pan Bin, the director of the county finance bureau, took the opportunity to collude with Zheng Chengyuan, the county magistrate, and falsely reported to the provincial government that the county's financial bureau's grain serials were lost due to the bandit disturbances, and that the year was also a year of famine, requesting exemption from this year's land tax. The provincial government was deceived and approved the exemption, while Pan Bin, the director of the finance bureau, still collected the taxes according to the number and filled his own pockets. The local people secretly reported to the provincial finance department, which sent Section Chief Qian Jiaxiang to investigate and found that it was true. He reported to Chairman Ye truthfully. Chairman Ye immediately sent Section Chief Qian to bring the guards Du Liangmo, Jiang Jinhuan, Li Huaizheng, Shen Yusheng, Li Zhengtin, Yan Guishan, etc. to Liyang to the county government to show the official documents and take Zheng Chengyuan, the county magistrate, Pan Bin, the director of the finance bureau, and the important corrupt officials Shen Zhiqing and Cao Qingzhi to the province. After the finance department inquired, it handed Pan, Shen, and Cao over to the guards for supervision. County Magistrate Zheng Chengyuan was supervised by two officials from the provincial government, Wang and Hu. They are currently residing in Room 30 of the Donglin Hotel, and the situation is very strict, but the treatment is still good.

Preparations for the Establishment of a Wheat Inspection Office: The Shanghai Agricultural Product Inspection Office, directly under the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines of the National Government, previously requested the Shanghai Flour Mill Association to ban the mixing of wheat with cement impurities and other malpractices. The Ministry of Agriculture and Mines approved the implementation of inspections. Jin Jiansi, the director of the Shanghai Inspection Office, believes that Wuxi is the center of Shanghai and Nanjing, and the volume of wheat exports and imports by land and water is very large. It is necessary to set up an office for inspection. He specially appointed Gu Fooki (a native of Wuxi) as the director of the Wuxi Inspection Office. Gu came to Wuxi the other day to actively prepare.

A Female Teacher Committed Suicide by Poisoning Before Her Wedding: Qian Yuying, a 17-year-old primary school teacher at the Nanyangli School in Guangfu Gate, is intelligent and beautiful. She currently lives with her maternal grandmother, Wu, on Dongxin Road. In April of this year, her maternal grandmother arranged for a matchmaker, Fei, to marry her to Guo, a merchant from Bashiqiao (Guo is 27 years old and works at the Gan Da Candle Shop outside the North Gate). At that time, a betrothal gift of 200 yuan was given, and it was stated that the marriage would take place in three years. However, in the summer, the Guo family suddenly sent a post through the matchmaker to choose yesterday as the date of the wedding. Qian Yuying expressed her dissatisfaction with the early wedding date. Her maternal grandmother immediately comforted her with kind words. Yesterday, the Guo family rented the Luchang Hotel on Hanchang Road as a wedding hall for the wedding. The wedding hall was filled with congratulatory guests and the bride's family prepared everything. Unexpectedly, Qian Yuying saw this situation and was extremely angry. She made an excuse to go out and bought a bottle of tranquilizer and returned home to secretly swallow it and close the door to sleep. The family members noticed and invited Dr. Zhu from the Brothers Hospital to the house to diagnose and administer two injections of a cardiotonic drug to turn the crisis into safety. At 9:00 in the evening, the Guo family took her away and completed the wedding in a hurry.

Changzhou

The River Port Merchant Corps Searches Bandit Dens: Banditry and kidnapping cases in the fifth district of Beizou, Wuyi County, have emerged one after another recently. The local people learned that the bandit dens were in Sanhuang Temple, Caijiatou, and Zoujiacun. The Sanhekou Merchant Corps discovered that bandit Xi Binggen was arrested by the Wucheng Joint Defense Office, and bandit Jin Yueliang confessed that Caijiatou was indeed a bandit den. The Sanhekou Merchant Corps organized a team to Caijiatou to search the other day, but the bandits had already fled after hearing the news. Only two quick guns and one box of bullets were found. A strict investigation is still underway.

Changshu

The Heads of Schools in the City Jointly Request Payment of Salaries: The Changshu education board has been owing salaries to the teachers and staff of schools for almost four and a half months. The accumulated arrears (from last year) amount to two and a half months, and the new arrears are about three months. It is difficult for most teachers to work on an empty stomach. Yesterday, the heads of schools in the city gathered at Siwen Elementary School to discuss methods for requesting payment of salaries. The heads of schools in the first district were also present. As a result, they first appealed to the education bureau and political party organs, and then recommended Lu Guanying from the preschool elementary school, Yang Junhe from the responsibility school, and Cao Jichang from the county junior high school as spokespersons. Then they went to the education bureau to petition. Director Gao Zishan extended an audience to the representatives and presented a petition. Director Gao repeatedly stated the difficulties and urged the principals to maintain their efforts. It is estimated that one or one and a half installments will be issued by the end of this month or the beginning of next month. The representatives then withdrew, and did not petition the party and government due to time constraints.

Jiangyin

Li Hongze's Case Awaits Disposition: Li Hongze, a former inspector of the Public Security Bureau, was reported by Xuan Xingbao to the Public Security Bureau for a gun case and for plotting to rob Shuiyue Nunnery with Xu Yun, Xu Yongliang, and Li Rongbao. The county interrogated him several times and sent Li Hongze and others to the provincial government for review. The provincial government then sent it back to the original Jiangyin County for interrogation. Yesterday (20th) afternoon, Xuan Xingbao was summoned and Li Hongze and the other three were brought to court. The interrogator Yang Cheng interrogated Xuan Xingbao. Xuan Xingbao confessed that they came to call for wine at the hotel. At Li Rongbao's house, he saw Xu Yun with a gun and only heard that they wanted to go to Shuiyue Nunnery. The rest he did not hear. When asked, Li Rongbao, Xu Yun, and Xu Yongliang claimed that they went to Shuiyue Nunnery to see a sky lantern and did not know whether it was a divine fire or a ghost fire. Li Hongze claimed that the gun was lost in the China Merchants Hotel and was picked up by Xu Yun. After the interrogation, the court ordered them to be sent elsewhere for disposition.

Wujiang

The Lianqie Case in Nanma Town is Solved: In the case of multiple robberies in Nanma Town in this county last month, the Yanmu Public Security Sub-bureau sent police to Wuzhen the other day to arrest six male and female suspects in the case. Two boxes of stolen goods, a large bag of clothes, and footgear were seized on the spot and sent to the county security bureau for review by the county government.

The Lake Survey Team Comes to the County: Sun Boqin, the head of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department's Great Lake Survey Team, led the entire team from Suzhou to the county yesterday to survey the entire line from Wuxian to Zhenze Town on the border of Zhejiang Province in this county. The entire line can be surveyed in about a week.

Zhenjiang

Opposition to the Chamber of Commerce's Collection of Electricity Surtax: The Suzhou-Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce plans to collect a surtax on electricity due to financial difficulties. After discussion, everyone believes that electricity is related to shops and households. It is against the law and violates the facts. The public unanimously opposes the electricity industry and does not recognize it. The Jiangsu Provincial Private Electricity Association has submitted a petition to the government requesting the Chamber of Commerce to find other ways to maintain the electricity industry.

Nantong

Lvsi Field Manager Reports Sea Banditry Infestation: The Lvsi Field Manager reports to the Lianghuai Salt Transportation Department that the sea bandits have landed and invaded Lvsi. The report states that Pan Kaiwu, Yan Zhenling, Song Lishan, etc., led 14 bandit ships with about 300-400 bandits fully armed and landed with unknown intentions. The field manager re-examined the facts and immediately joined with local agencies to step up prevention. It was found that the bandits were either on ships or on the shore with unsettled movements. They also posted a notice claiming to be Song Lishan, the director of the Fisheries Protection Office of the Chinese Red Army. It was recently heard that Shen Guanxi led more than ten bandit ships to anchor in the ocean, wanting to fight against Pan, Yan, Song, and other bandits. The two groups of sea bandits are more than ten miles apart and are preparing for war. Recently, the Songhu Bandit Suppression Headquarters has ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Security Department to suppress them.

The Head of the County Court is Changed: Dong Banggan, the head of the Nantong County Court, was transferred by the Ministry of Justice to be a judge of the High Court Branch, and Jian Kuiyang was appointed to replace him. Jian took office on the 20th.

Request for Punishment of Trouble-Making Thugs: Thugs in Xingan Town, Langshan District, gathered to loot weapons and burn houses. The military police arrested Gu Daxing and other four people on the spot and sent them to the county. After the military and political commission tried them, they were submitted to the higher authorities for punishment.

Yangzhou

The Province Orders the Construction of an Airport: The Jiangdu County Government received an order from the province yesterday that the bandit forces in northern Jiangsu were rampant. The headquarters approved the allocation of two aircraft to assist in the suppression of bandits. The telegram ordered Yangzhou to quickly find an open field for landing. After receiving the order, Chen, the county magistrate, ordered the Public Security Bureau to search. It is now heard that the director of the Public Security Bureau, Chen Lu, and the former president of the Aviation Promotion Association, Wang Jingting, have been instructed to handle the matter. It has now been determined that the Dajiaochang outside the West Gate will be the landing site and a map has been drawn and submitted to the county for approval.

Fugitive's Private Possession of Guns Affects Neighbors: The Criminal Investigation Team of the County Police Force received a tip that Zhou Er, one of the large number of fugitives from the detention center, had returned home (living in Jiangwang Temple). The team's criminal investigators secretly went to the place to arrest him. Unexpectedly, Zhou had already fled to another place with his family. The officers found a long gun in the canopy near the surname's residence and took the owner of the canopy, Wen, back to the headquarters for review.

Two Public Security Bureau Directors Accused: Party member Yin Shangbai reported to the county that the directors of the 80th and 2nd Public Security Bureaus were protecting opium dens and collecting fees privately. The county has ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate and reply. It is also heard that the director of the 6th Public Security Bureau embezzled more than 300 yuan in fines and swallowed the August salary. The September salary was issued only after the August police salary was withheld, which caused dissatisfaction among the long-term police and they filed a complaint with the superiors.

Jiashan

Shops Around the Sunhui Bridge Petition for Reconstruction: The shops on the east and west sides of Sunhui Bridge outside the east gate of this county are lined up and are a prosperous area. Now, in order to facilitate transportation by rickshaw, the county government has dismantled the old-fashioned bridges one after another. However, due to limited funds, it has not been possible to completely rebuild them, and only the bridge abutments have been paved on the original bridge foundation to allow vehicles to pass, so that the bridge abutments are higher than the ground, which covers the shops on both sides and hinders business. The Sunhui Bridge is now also being dismantled. It started demolition the other day, but the bridge body is too high and the bridge abutments are too high from the ground. At a moderate point, it is more than two feet, so that more than 20 shops are covered. Therefore, the merchants raised hundreds of yuan to completely dismantle and rebuild the bridge to avoid the shops being covered by the bridge abutments and hindering business. They have reported the situation to the county government for instructions.

Jiaxing

Telegraph Request to Send Personnel for Re-Inspection of Bridges: The Jiao and Zhi Bridges in Jiaxing County were proposed by the County Construction Bureau and approved by the County Construction Committee for renovation and construction. The construction has been completed and the county has submitted a request to the Construction Department to send personnel for acceptance. The Construction Department has sent Zhou to Jiaxing for acceptance. It is now learned that the County Executive Committee believes that although the construction of the two bridges has been completed, they do not conform to the design drawings, which makes the bridge openings smaller than the original, making it difficult for boats to pass and causing river blockage. This is very important to the residents' drinking water. Therefore, the 53rd meeting resolved to telegraph the Provincial Executive Committee to telegraph the Provincial Government to quickly order the Construction Department to send civil engineering specialists with rich experience to Jiaxing to conduct a re-inspection with representatives of various groups to emphasize construction.

Call for Overlapping Surtaxes on Land Tax: The surtaxes added to the Jiaxing land tax compensation have long exceeded the limits set by the ministry. This year, five jiao for district autonomous administrative expenses and six jiao for land consolidation expenses have been added to the land tax compensation, making it even more difficult for the people to bear. Therefore, local citizens Sheng Yuan and Zhang Baoming have submitted petitions to the Finance Department, the Provincial Government, and the Executive Yuan and Finance Department of the National Government calling for the abolition. They have received a reply from the Ministry of Finance that it has ordered the Zhejiang Finance Department to order the county government to convene local public groups to publicly assess land prices and calculate whether the normal and surtaxes under the land tax exceed 1% of the land price. Sheng Yuan and others submitted a petition to the Finance Department the other day requesting that it quickly order the Jiaxing County Government to convene a public land price meeting of local public groups.

Huzhou

Bandits Robbed Four Boats: On the 18th, six bandits speaking Henan dialect were suddenly discovered in the Wushanjian Bridge area of Changxing County. Each held a wooden-cased gun and waited by the bridge to rob passing boats. That day, Wu and others' rice boats returning from selling rice, as well as candle core boats and civilian boats, were robbed. The bandits forced all the boats to stop and searched them one by one. All the silver dollars were swept away, resulting in a loss of about 200 yuan, and the candle core passengers were kidnapped.

Xu Jinsheng Beaten His Younger Brother to Death with a Carrying Pole: Xu Jinsheng, a resident of Fugu, outside the south gate of Changxing, suddenly quarreled with his younger brother, Ahe, the other day. They first started with a quarrel and then resorted to violence. After neighbors persuaded them to stop, Ahe complained to his neighbor, Qiu Caifa. When Jinsheng learned of this, he took a carrying pole and ambushed in front of Qiu's house. Not long after, Ahe came out of Qiu's house, and Jinsheng used the carrying pole to hit Ahe's waist several times in a row. After being hit, Ahe endured the pain and fled back to Qiu Caifa's house. However, Ahe's internal injuries were too severe and he died despite medical treatment.

Hangzhou

The Construction Department Promotes Housing for the Poor in Various Counties: The Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, in view of the increasing population and the scarcity of housing in recent years, and the fact that landlords are harshly increasing rents and arbitrarily oppressing tenants, is seeking to remedy the situation in order to relieve the suffering of tenants in various counties. It has decided to build dozens of houses in each county at a low price for rent. The construction funds will be allocated from local public funds, and the rent collected will be used as public fund interest and house repair fees. The construction affairs will be presided over by the County Property Committee and assisted by the county government. The department has ordered the county magistrates to plan in earnest.

The Maritime Administration Bureau Established a Provincial Shipyard: The Zhejiang Maritime Administration Bureau believes that, apart from steamships, most of the other civilian ships in the province are built by private shipyards that stick to old methods and have no innovation. Therefore, it has been unable to fully facilitate water transportation. Therefore, it is now planning to establish a larger shipyard to improve the construction of sailing ships on the one hand and to repair the damage of motor ships on the other. It will be established as soon as 80,000 yuan has been raised and will be located on the border of Zhenhai.

Xiaoshan

Disputes over Rent Estimation and Harvest in Tenancy: The early and late rice harvests in the southern township of Xiaoshan this year have been very abundant. Regardless of high or low fields, the actual grain harvest is more than four dan. However, the tenants are only willing to estimate the maximum harvest at three dan. The owners naturally do not care about this, so disputes arise frequently. Both tenants and owners have asked the party and county authorities for a solution.

The Provincial Committee Thoroughly Investigates the Complaint Case: Li Yuan, the director of the Linpu Public Security Sub-bureau in Xiaoshan, was previously accused of various misdeeds by merchants Zhao Zhenqi, Lu Huaiqing, Tang Jie Mei, and Shen Che, etc. to the provincial government. The province ordered Xiaoshan County to investigate and reply to each item. Recently, the Department of Civil Affairs believed that the case was still untrue, so it commissioned Lou Zhenghua, a new political instructor from the Department of Civil Affairs, to investigate each item thoroughly and report back to the province.

Two Families in the Southern Township Robbed in One Night: Wei Amao and Zhang Yu's families, residents of the southern township of Xiaoshan in the villages of Heshangdian and Zhangcun, were known for their wealth. At 12:00 on the night of the 17th, a group of bandits suddenly came with a large number of people, speaking various dialects, with torches and sticks, and broke into the door. First, they robbed Wei Amao's house and then the family of Zhang Yu in the same village was also robbed. The search lasted about two hours before the thieves left with their loot to the south. It is said that after the two families checked, they lost about 2,000 yuan worth of soft valuables and clothes.

Ningbo

Chairman Chiang's Return to Fenghua: Since the news of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's return to his ancestral home in Fenghua, Jiang Jieqing, the director of Ningbo Customs, and Mao Bingli, the director of the Public Security Bureau, went to Beijing together to ask for instructions on the itinerary. Jiang and Mao returned to Ningbo from Beijing yesterday. It is said that unless there are special circumstances, they will return to Ningbo around the 20th of this month. After Jiang, the director, returns to Ningbo, he will go to Fenghua to arrange the welcome.

Resolution to Raise 120,000 Yuan: The Yinxian County Government held an administrative meeting yesterday and decided to raise 120,000 yuan in county public funds to compensate for the 19th-year local budget of 20,000 yuan and to build a second-line county road. The right to inspect cannot be abandoned. Binner Harn, the British Consul General in Shanghai, who also serves as the Ningbo Consul, sent a letter yesterday to the Zhenhai Fortress Headquarters requesting the withdrawal of armed soldiers inspecting the Xin Beijing ship. The headquarters refused after the letter, stating that its responsibility was to prevent chaos and maintain security.

Political Program of the Chinese Nationalist Party

Article 6 of the Domestic Policy: Guarantee complete freedom of assembly, association, speech, publication, residence, and belief for the people.

Article 4 of the Domestic Policy: Implement universal suffrage and abolish class elections based on property as a standard.

Article 7 and Article 8 of the Domestic Policy: Strictly stipulate the statutory amount of land tax and ground tax, prohibit all extra levies such as Likin, etc., and abolish all of them.

Article 12 of the Domestic Policy: Confirm in law, economics, education, and society the principle of equality between men and women and promote the development of women's rights.

Article 9 of the Domestic Policy: Clear up the household registration, reorganize the arable land, and adjust the production and marketing of grain to seek equality in food for the people.

Important News in Education

Expanding Turmoil at Central University

Students Present Eighteen Demands

Alumni Association Unanimously Supports Demands

School Administration to be Reorganized

Zhang Zuoshi Forced to Leave the School

Since Central University students Tu Juyiao and 290 others voiced corrective opinions regarding the school's recent facilities, demanding reform in school affairs, it has aroused unanimous sympathy from the entire faculty, students, and alumni. The movement to improve school affairs is expanding daily. The following records yesterday's news:

(1) Six Hundred Students, Including Xu Zicheng, Make Demands. Yesterday, more than six hundred students, including Xu Zicheng, addressed a letter to the school president, continuing the spirit of Tu Juyiao, putting forward eighteen demands: (1) Immediately determine a school operating plan; (2) Reduce all economic burdens on students, such as donation fees and experiment fees, which should be immediately waived. Tuition and dormitory fees should be appropriately reduced; (3) Improve classrooms and student dormitories to emphasize hygiene; (4) Thoroughly investigate corrupt and despicable elements such as Zhang Wei; (5) Thoroughly investigate the nationalistic faction led by Zou Bingwen and the reorganization faction led by Lin Qun, to strictly enforce party-led education; (6) Reorganize the school affairs council to implement the spirit of professor-led school governance; (7) Appoint deans of each college as soon as possible; (8) Hire more full-time professors, emphasize talent selection, and increase compensation; (9) Maximize acceptance of public opinion; (10) Rectify the publication enterprise to demonstrate Central University's spirit of academic pursuit; (11) Determine independent funding for each college; (12) Reduce all administrative expenses; (13) Increase funding for books; (14) Publicize the budget and final accounts, implementing open finances; (15) Implement an academic scholarship system; (16) Increase compensation for student service in the headquarters; (17) Encourage teacher-student cooperation; (18) Promote academic studies and establish research institutes.

(2) The Alumni Association Unanimously Supports. The alumni associations of National Southeastern University, National Ginling University, and National Central University held a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members at Central University at 8 PM yesterday (the 20th). In addition to the full attendance of the executive and supervisory committee members, several alumni such as Zhou Houxu attended. Chairman Jiang Jiaxiang resolved that, out of love for their alma mater, they unanimously supported the on-campus students' movement to improve school affairs and selected Jiang Jiaxiang, Yu Xilai, Chen Xiexun, Chen Shizhen, and Peng Baichuan to draft a letter to the president in accordance with the main points of today's resolution.

(3) The School Changes its Administrative Organization. The school's administrative organization, which operates under the president and is divided into three departments: secretary, academic affairs, and general affairs, costing 300,000 yuan annually, is one of the focal points of student criticism. The school authorities, having accepted the students' suggestions for improvement, decided to abolish the three departments of secretary, academic affairs, and general affairs, and reorganize them into a general affairs office, headed by Chief of Academic Affairs Huang Pu Huan. The General Affairs Office is divided into five sections: registration, documentation, publication, accounting, and general services. The original editorial matters are incorporated into the publication section, and construction projects are incorporated into the general services section.

(4) The President Prohibits Anonymous Posters. Recently, students at the school, citing poor school affairs, put forward several suggestions for improvement and submitted them to the president for adoption, while simultaneously issuing a publicity outline to draw the attention of all students. In addition, some students took this opportunity to post anonymous notices and leaflets everywhere, arbitrarily attacking all inappropriate measures taken by the school. President Zhang Naiyan therefore issued a proclamation strictly prohibiting such actions in order to maintain school discipline.

(5) Zhang Zuoshi Forced to Leave the School. Secretary-General Zhang Zuoshi, opposed by the students, hastily left the school yesterday to return to Hangzhou. President Zhang Naiyan has retained the accounting director Dai Chongen and general affairs director Shao Cong, in order to avoid a shutdown of school affairs.

Overview of Education in Dongtai County

The Jiangsu Provincial Office for Joint Preparation of Compulsory Education recently reported the results of a survey on the status of education in Dongtai County. An abstract of the original text is recorded below: Dongtai County has suffered consecutive years of famine in the past two years. Fortunately, the efforts of educational administrative personnel have kept the arrears to a minimum. Now, Director Xu Yipeng is determined to rectify the situation, and the budget for this year has already been established, with the addition of 19 urban and rural schools. Social education has also been promoted, and recent attention has been paid to recovering temple and school properties to serve as the foundation for the future development of education throughout the county. It has been found that the temple and school properties total more than 28,000 mu, located over 100 li northeast of the county seat. Originally, they were the wasteland of the Temple of Literature and community schools, but were later occupied by the Tong Sui Company. Various local public organizations believe that these properties belong to education, and according to precise information, they have separately requested the provincial government to recover the property rights. Recently, after a provincial government meeting, the county was ordered to safeguard the total rent and grain, awaiting resolution. If fully recovered, the cotton income from last year amounts to more than 180,000 yuan, calculated at 9 yuan per mu, which will be of great importance to the future development of education in the county. (1) Regarding the income of expenses for the 19th year, the regular items such as surtaxes and collected installments amounted to 65,636 yuan, miscellaneous taxes and surtaxes amounted to 11,260 yuan, special donations amounted to 5,793 yuan, miscellaneous donations amounted to 111,902 yuan, property funds amounted to 40,824 yuan, and tuition and lodging fees amounted to 7,872 yuan. Temporary items such as field and house mortgages amounted to 50 yuan, totaling 148,287 yuan. Regarding expenditures, educational administrative fees amounted to 11,595 yuan, general education expenses amounted to 26,536 yuan, vocational education expenses amounted to 56,402 yuan, social education expenses amounted to 22,200 yuan, special income amounted to 5,850 yuan, and special expenses were the same. The first reserve fund was 7,295 yuan, and the second reserve fund was 21,870 yuan. This is a rough outline of income and expenditure. Regarding the safekeeping of funds, in addition to the bureau's own income, a temporary management committee is established for the educational funds of each city and township, with the local educational committee member serving as an ex officio member and an additional three to five members appointed. Their duties are: 1. To manage the educational base property fund of the city or township; 2. To collect all educational funds; 3. To distribute funds according to the budget of the Education Bureau; 4. To raise educational funds; 5. To supervise the collection of educational funds levied by the authorities. Since the implementation of this system, the benefits have been clear: 1. The principals of each city and township thoroughly understand the contents of educational expenses; 2. The expenses of each rural school are distributed by the educational committee of each district, sparing each school the trouble of going to the bureau to receive funds; 3. The educational base property fund is easier to manage in districts and can avoid corruption; 4. When educational expenses are difficult, each district raises its own funds, which are smaller in amount and easier to handle; 5. The principals of each city and township, because of their own relationship with the city and township's educational expenses, can assist in the safekeeping and fundraising of property. Therefore, even after two years of rare famine, Dongtai County has accumulated little in arrears in education expenses, and even when there are arrears, each school has been genuinely forgiven, resulting in very few disputes. Since the 16th year of the Republic, the educational expenses of various counties have been centralized in succession to seek uniformity, but the actual difficulties are still numerous. Now, Dongtai County has adopted a district-based management method for educational expenses, which, although slightly different from other counties, does not hinder its implementation and has yielded results. This is truly a research material for those who pay attention to local educational funding. (2) Compulsory education is divided into six school districts throughout the county, with a population of 1,136,142 people. There are a total of 110 public and private primary schools with 183 grades. A total of 6,876 school-age children have been enrolled, and 181,544 have not been enrolled. The county high school's rural normal department is the old site of the former Muli Normal School. The school buildings are in good condition, and running a rural normal school is especially appropriate. The county's teachers are comprised of 8,000 normal school students, 36 graduates of A-level normal schools, 12 graduates of three-year normal schools, 1 graduate of four-year normal schools, 1 kindergarten teacher, 4 post-secondary and high school teachers, and 70 unqualified teachers. The teacher resources seem to be lacking. Each district has set up a rural experimental primary school. If the gains from the experiment can become the center of education in a village, the results will be significant. There are 14 private primary schools in each school district. At a time when educational funds are stretched, the gradual increase in private primary schools is not necessarily a major boost. The current distribution of compulsory education funds allocates 7,800 yuan for reorganizing old undertakings, 16,000 yuan for new undertakings, and 2,576 yuan for accumulated funds. With the vast territory of the county and the large number of out-of-school children, increasing fundraising and promotion cannot be delayed. (3) General education in the city includes a county-run junior high school with 120 students in three grades and a budget of 5,500 yuan (with an attached rural normal course of one grade with 40 students and a budget of 2,000 yuan, plus 1,200 yuan for food).

Principal Liu Peiyuan has a total of 16 faculty and staff. There are a total of 24 complete primary schools (including 5 private schools), with 33 grades and the number of students is highest in Pingcha Primary School. Experimental primary schools and girls' primary schools also have more than 300 students. Pengcha City has a private junior high school. (4) Social education has progressed rapidly in recent years thanks to the efforts of Director Xu and Wang Xintian, head of the social education section. A public education center has been established in each of the urban areas of Pengcha and Shiyan, and a farmers' education center has been established in Xixi. Nineteen public schools are specially run, each with 40 yuan per term. An experimental public education area has also been established in the city, with three grades of adult, women, and kindergarten public schools with many students. Other facilities such as reading rooms and specially contracted public tea gardens have also been established one after another. Recently, an experimental mobile public school has been planned, and government agencies below the county government have also organized the Dongtai County Government Directly Subordinate Agencies Public School Promotion Committee. The public schools that should be established by each agency can open soon (remainder omitted).

Ministry of Education Sends Guo Youshou to Attend the Industry and Commerce Conference

The Industry and Commerce Conference is scheduled to be held in Beijing from November 1st to 8th. The Ministry of Education recently appointed Guo Youshou, section chief of the Higher Education Department, as its representative to attend the conference.

Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School Exhibits Teachers' Achievements

The Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School on Shangwen Road has been reorganized for three years since 1927. During normal times, it has spared no effort in experimenting with and researching new education. There are more than fifty reports and publications on experimental research work, which is considered one of the most diligent elementary schools in recent times. Today (the 22nd) is the anniversary of the school's reorganization. A joint commemorative ceremony was held with Shanghai Middle School in the morning. In the afternoon, achievements were exhibited at the school and a recreational assembly was held. It is reported that the achievements on display are mostly teachers' works, divided into four rooms: administration, teaching, research, and cultivation. Administrative achievements are divided into plans, regulations, and forms. Teaching achievements are divided into methods, materials, and equipment. Research achievements are divided into published and unpublished works. Cultivation achievements are divided into party ideology research, reading reports, and leisure life. The recreational assembly focuses on performances in various subjects and is different from those that lean towards singing and dancing.

Wu Song Public Sports Field, 3 PM Today

Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts Organizes Alumni Association

The Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts is the first art school in China, and it has been nineteen years since its founding. The president is Liu Haisu, and over the years, there have been five to six thousand alumni. Most of those currently engaged in art in society, those who have founded art schools in various provinces and counties, those who hold art positions in secondary schools in various provinces and counties, and those who study art in France and Japan are alumni of the school. However, there has long been a lack of liaison organizations, which has prevented the concentration of efforts. Recently, Acting President Wang Yuanbo and Dean of Academic Affairs Ding Yuan of the school, in view of this, have initiated the Alumni Association and are actively proceeding. It is reported that the first preparatory committee meeting is scheduled to be held today, and the founding congress is planned to be held in late November on the school's anniversary.

Shanghai Art College Travels to West Lake

The Shanghai Art College on Jiangwan Road has a vibrant spirit and excellent achievements, opening a new chapter for the art world in China. Recently, the new campus has been completed and famous professors such as Chen Baoyi, Chen Zhibu, Ni Huayi, Shu Zhen, Wulanman, Li Cuizhen, Wu Bochao, Ye Qiuyuan, and Liu Banzhu have been hired, who are also extremely popular with students. Because the graduation date of the Class A students of the three-year Western Medicine Department is approaching, professors Chen Baoyi, Ni Huayi, and others are leading a study tour to West Lake with approximately 40 male and female students. They departed on the 20th and will spend approximately three weeks there. It is reported that the school president, Wang Daoyuan, will also go to guide them in the coming days.

National Games Open in Japan

The 17th National Games will be held on the 25th of this month. In preparation for participating in the World Games in two years, Japan is intensifying its track and field competitions. All competition rules are in accordance with the Olympic system. Low hurdles have been changed to 400 meters, medium hurdles, and the shot put has been changed to 16 pounds, with the addition of a weight throw. Because the players participating in the European Games have all returned to the country, it has been decided to hold the 17th National Games in Osaka on the 25th and 26th of this month to select new talent and encourage future generations to compete internationally throughout the year. After the completion of this conference, the Meiji Jingu Sports Tournament will be held in Tokyo. It is also one of the National Games of Japan, and its scope is larger than the ordinary one. In addition to the eight championships, there will also be equestrian, rowing, anndao, martial arts, boxing, sumo wrestling, gymnastics, and other events. In addition to students and citizens, all military camps and police stations must participate. Japan holds an average of three or four national games each year. Before the Far Eastern Games this year, the 17th Games were held once. The opening of this tournament is also imminent. Japan will also send players to participate in the China-Japan Joint Games in November this year. This conference is sponsored by the Kwantung Government and sponsored by Director Zhang. It is held alternately in Dalian and Lushun every year. However, because the Japanese underestimate the level of track and field in our country, I am afraid that they will not send first-class players to participate at that time. Japan is preparing for the above-mentioned major conferences, so pre-selection competitions are being held in the country. The Kinki pre-selection competition was completed in the past two days. Kinki includes Osaka, Kobe, Kyoto, Nagoya, Nara, Wakayama, and other counties.

Municipal Elementary School Joint Games

Baseball Throw Rules

The Shanghai Municipal Elementary School Third Joint Games are scheduled to be held from November 12th to 14th. Details of various regulations and methods were issued to each school by the Municipal Education Bureau yesterday. The sports events are generally the same as in the previous games, but in the track and field competition, the girls' basketball throw has been changed to a baseball throw. The baseball throw rules set by the association are as follows:

1. Ball Used: The ball used in the competition shall be a standard 12-inch circumference indoor baseball. 2. Throwing Line: A wooden board at least 7 centimeters (4 and ¾ inches) wide and 3.66 meters (12 feet) long shall be buried flat in the ground. The inner edge of this board shall be the throwing line. 3. Throwing Method: When throwing the baseball, the player must hold the ball with one hand behind the throwing line and throw it forward from behind the shoulder. The action is the same as the outfield baseball throw. 4. Foul: Either of the following two situations in the competition shall be deemed as a failed throw without the need for measurement: (A) Violation of Article 3; (B) During the throw, any part of the body or clothing touches the throwing line or the ground outside the line before the ball lands. 5. Number of Attempts: Each competitor throws three times and the scores of the top six players are used. They may then throw three more times, using the longest of these as the competition score. 6. Error: A fault line is drawn one meter from the throwing line. A competitor stepping out or running past this line without throwing will be counted as an error. Two errors count as one failed attempt. If the player throws the ball without running, 7. Measurement: The measurement of the baseball is done with a right angle measuring from the nearest point where the baseball lands to the throwing line or its extended line.
