Medical News and Notes

Dr. Wang Rongzhi, a female physician, has returned to Shanghai from North China and has now established the Baojian Obstetrics and Gynecology Hospital at No. 17 Scotta Road. Ms. Wang is a graduate of the Tokyo Japanese Obstetrics School designated by the Japanese Ministry of Internal Affairs. She has served as a physician in Japanese hospitals in Dalian and Harbin for many years and has a wealth of experience.

Physician Yang Zhongfu's clinic on Guizhou Road will be demolished, and he has now moved to No. 509 Dashunli, diagonally opposite the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road. Clinic hours remain the same.

Bureau of Public Health Revokes Xu Jianquan's Denture License

Xu Jianquan, the owner of the Xu Jianquan Denture Shop at No. 85 Oujia Road, had registered with the Municipal Bureau of Public Health and obtained a denture license. Recently, for unknown reasons, he leased the shop to Li Yuanhua and privately transferred the denture license. Li Yuanhua then continued to operate the business under the false pretense of the license. This was discovered by the Bureau of Public Health sanitation inspector. Li Yuanhua, knowing that he had violated the regulations, bribed the sanitation inspector in an attempt to escape punishment. The sanitation inspector was unmoved and brought Li Yuanhua, along with Xu Jianquan's denture license, to the police station for interrogation. The director of the station fined him 30 yuan. Xu Jianquan's denture license was revoked by the Bureau of Public Health.

Fourth Preparatory Meeting of the Hongshun Mutual Aid Society

The Hongshun Mutual Aid Society held its fourth meeting yesterday. The meeting was conducted according to etiquette. Chairman Yang Wendao reported on the following matters: (A) The association has now received Batch No. 3040 from the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, approving its registration and establishment. Therefore, it will hold an election establishment meeting on October 26. In addition to inviting senior successors to participate in guidance, it will also request the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs and the Municipal Civil Training Committee to send personnel to guide the election establishment. All internal meeting procedures and staff have been arranged. It is hoped that the grand color will illuminate the charitable social group with great prospects. It is hoped that all comrades will respect themselves. (B) Each member is planning to be issued a membership certificate with all the association's constitution printed on it for inspection, pending the Executive Committee's decision to issue it and recover the cost of 1 dime per certificate. (C) Yang Wendao read the constitution aloud to the public. The rights of male and female members are quite equal and treated equally. When the member's own parents, wife, or husband pass away, they have the right to receive a funeral allowance. It was decided that each funeral allowance would be 100 yuan, plus 20 yuan for carriage expenses. However, it must be verified by a dispatched investigator before it can be issued. As for the marriage of members, a gift of 4 yuan will be sent, and then 2 yuan will be sent to celebrate the birth of a son or daughter to express congratulations. (D) If a member dies in another city, his or her family members may guarantee to receive the funeral allowance, but if the whole family leaves the city, the family members shall not send anything other than incense money of 2 yuan to express condolences. (E) If a member encounters an unexpected misfortune, all members should provide maintenance fees of 5 dimes per person to provide relief for urgent needs. This payment shall be paid to the accountant within one period for the formal establishment of the General Assembly. The meeting was adjourned after the motion was passed.

News from Various Labor Unions

The Western-style Woodworking Industry Labor Union held its fourth supplementary citywide representative conference yesterday. With the exception of Mao Quantai from Bazishan, all members were present. Chairman Zhou Maoshan performed the opening ceremony as usual. After the chairman's report, the election began immediately. The results were as follows: Zhao Daolin with 40 votes, Huang Zhengzhong with 37 votes, Zhou Pinxiang with 35 votes, Zhou Maoshan with 32 votes, Hong Zongliang with 31 votes, Zheng Yongshou with 31 votes, and Yuan Fuyun with 30 votes were elected as directors. Sun Pingqiao with 30 votes, Zhu Bingyao with 28 votes, and Zhu Jigang with 27 votes were elected as alternate directors. Wu Jimei with 30 votes, Zhou Xingchu with 29 votes, and Zhu Yunbiao with 23 votes were elected as supervisors. Zhou Rongfang with 23 votes and Li Changrui with 20 votes were elected as alternate supervisors. After the election, discussions began on: (1) A proposal to request higher authorities to approve amendments to the agreement and improve treatment, which was approved; (2) How to handle those who do not join the union or pay fees, which was decided to persuade non-members to join and to handle non-payers according to regulations; (3) How to deal with employers extending working hours, which was resolved that workers should unite and stop work according to the stipulated hours in the agreement, and if employers take drastic actions, request higher authorities for protection; (4) Responsible personnel of the union should be responsible for weekly duties, which was decided that in addition to the chairman and executive director being stationed at the union hall regularly, three people should take turns to the union hall every night from 6 PM to 9 PM to handle union affairs, unless there are special circumstances, and if the month ends on the 31st, the secretary should assist on that night, and those who are absent without reason will be disciplined. After the discussion, slogans were shouted, and the meeting adjourned.

Wang Lide, a representative from the Citizen Training Association, delivered a report on (1) the fourth session's union affairs and financial report, (2) guidance from upper-level representatives and guests, and (3) the reelection of the fifth session's directors. The mediation section proposed that many factories are closing down and the livelihood of workers is cut off, and a solution should be determined quickly, which was resolved to (1) submit a request to higher authorities and (2) engage in registration and propaganda. The propaganda section proposed that because the branches of each factory have little publicity, a small number of members are not familiar with the union rules, and a "Labor Voice Monthly" should be published quickly to facilitate publicity, which was approved. The union plans to hold regular meetings every Wednesday at 6 PM, and this resolution was approved.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that there is a low-pressure system in western China, causing cloudy skies in the Yangtze River basin. There are gentle winds over Shandong and the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. A low-pressure system will pass through Mongolia and move towards the southeast east. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 72.0 degrees and the lowest was 48.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 63.4 degrees and the lowest was 44.2 degrees.

Letters

To the Editorial Department of the Local News Section of the Shen Bao: Having read today's edition of your newspaper's local news column, "Important News from the Shipping Industry: Application for a Pilot's License," some details do not entirely align with the facts. The following clarifications are provided: (1) Mr. Liu Fupei's diploma and certificates are complete and were submitted to our association on the 16th of this month. (2) Mr. Yu Jianfu was recommended by Mr. Liu Shisun, a member of our association's executive committee. (3) The submission to the Ministry and the letter were not handled simultaneously. We kindly request prompt correction to align with the facts. Respectfully submitted, Shanghai Shipping Association, 19.10.21

To the Editors of the Shen Bao: Cai Zhen, because of the Xu Zhuoran assassination case, came to Hangzhou and is now awaiting trial and has not been arrested. The content published in your newspaper's local news column on October 19th is a misreport and should be corrected. Sincerely, Ye Cai Zhen, October 19, Year 19. Yesterday, I read in your newspaper a news item about a man from Nantong, Xu Yixi, who drowned himself. After investigating, there were many inaccuracies. The corrections are as follows: The deceased was Xu Yilan, also known as Hu Hou, from Jinsha, Nantong. He used to make ropes for a living at his mother's place. On the 14th of this month, he went from Tong to Xu Gengsheng's place at 909 Huaji Road. The next day, Xu Gengsheng took him to the home of his cousin, Xu Guangsheng, for one night, and Jiang Guang led him to the printing office on the kiln in Zhabei, where he was given chrysanthemums. On the 18th, the news of his drowning came out. Whether the deceased committed suicide has not yet been confirmed. His father is now in Nantong, and a letter has been sent to inform him. Once his father comes to Shanghai or has additional information, we will inform you again. Hereby, a letter is sent to your newspaper's local news editing department for correction. Xu Guangsheng, cousin of the deceased.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Sea Guest

Husband: Oh dear, where did all these books come from, and why are they all about economics?

Wife: Didn't you tell me last week that managing a household requires understanding economics? So, I spent my entire monthly allowance on economics books.

Husband: Oh my, I meant to tell you to be more frugal.

Wife: Who told you to beat around the bush?

Customer: Today's steak is too tough, not as good as last time.

Waiter: Sir, you must be mistaken. You certainly didn't eat here last time.

Woman A: Last night, I sang at a concert and had great success. My voice was excellent and filled the hall.

Woman B: Yes, I was there last night too and saw many guests getting up and leaving halfway through. Most of them were probably giving up their seats to allow your voice to fill the hall.

Woman (bumped into by a man striding confidently with chest puffed out): Sir, where are your eyes? Why are you walking into people?

Man: How rude! Why do you call me "sir"? Don't you know I'm a local official here?

A Record of the Moving of Former President Tan's Remains

— Zheng Lugeng

Several weeks have passed since the passing of Tan Gong, President of the Executive Yuan. Heaven did not spare us, taking away our elder statesman, and the country is in mourning, with shock both at home and abroad. The Central Government, remembering his meritorious service, specially appointed a commissioner to organize the funeral committee and issued the National Funeral Law and National Funeral Ceremony procedures to show the Party and the nation's intention to reward merit and promote thrift. After the National Day celebration, the remains were moved to the First Park. On that day, the ceremony was solemn and extremely sorrowful. Notables of the Party and the nation arrived early at the Tan family's residence to await the carrying of the coffin. Plain cars and white horses followed one after another. Along the way, the security was tight, with guards standing watch, and the citizens who waited on the roadside numbered in the tens of thousands, creating a scene of empty streets. Around 9 AM, after the floral tributes and public memorial, the cannon was fired to begin the moving of the remains. Amidst the throng of heads, the funeral banner fluttered, and mournful music resonated. Tang Ke's vehicle led the way, followed by the commander-in-chief, Gu Zhenglun, leading each line in an orderly procession. First was the army honor guard, a company of cavalry holding spears and pressing their reins, followed by a full regiment of infantry carrying guns and proceeding slowly. Next was the navy honor guard, followed by the police honor guard, with vehicles and horses interspersed, creating an extremely somber scene. Then, representatives from various places who came to escort the remains advanced in order, forming the fifth line, numbering several tens of groups, proceeding in a meandering fashion. All the staff of the Executive Yuan wore blue robes and black vests made of domestic goods, while female staff members wore blue cloth qipaos, creating a solemn atmosphere. Military and political departments and other military organizations were fully armed, while others wore either Chinese or Western attire, all conveying a sense of sighing and grief within a solemn and quiet atmosphere. The sixth line consisted of Party, government, and military leaders, foreign guests, relatives, and family members holding the ropes attached to the coffin. The hearse was Executive Yuan vehicle number 104, which Tan Gong had used during his lifetime, with a portrait of Tan Gong hanging inside, and four of his beloved horses leading the way, decorated with red brocade ropes several feet long. Chiang Kai-shek, in military uniform, held the front rope, his expression filled with sorrow, reflecting the deep pain of losing a close friend. The rest followed in their respective ranks, holding the ropes. The seventh line consisted of the coffin and the funeral vehicles escorting the remains. The coffin was covered with pure black satin, with the Party flag and national flag draped over it, without ornate decorations. Sixty-four pallbearers in plain clothes with blue edges alternated in carrying the coffin. The family members wore black mourning attire to show their endless filial piety. The three daughters of the deceased rode in one carriage, followed by the eldest daughter-in-law, a Westerner, riding in another carriage, their faces stained with tears, showing that the "Liao E" poem should not be abandoned. The eighth line was a cavalry squad bringing up the rear. From evening until the end, only the sound of horses' hooves, the sound of footsteps, the sound of solemn orders, and the sound of the wings of the planes circling in the sky to protect the remains could be heard, creating a scene of solemnity and grief. Oh, how great! Before each honor guard squad, there was a mounted officer in charge of command and discipline. In addition, each line had a band leading the way, infantry bringing up the rear, boy scouts maintaining order, and motorcycles patrolling back and forth. After about an hour, they arrived at the mourning hall to enshrine the remains and perform the public memorial service, and then dispersed. Recording the main points of the event, one cannot help but feel the sorrow of the mountain collapsing and the tree decaying. (To be continued)

Yang Xingfo's Avian Obsession

— Lean Sheep

I recently read in a newspaper a story about Yang Xingfo, a prominent figure in the Party and former Vice President of the University Council, stating that Mr. Yang had a fondness for horses and often prepared two fine steeds in Beijing, riding them to the suburbs at dawn, and sincerely welcoming anyone, whether known or unknown, to ride alongside him. This reminded me of what my friend Zhang Jun told me, that Mr. Yang not only loved horses but also liked to raise birds, such as thrushes, white-feathered parrots, and more, up to a dozen species, all of which were cherished and played with by Mr. Yang. When he was at home, he would often use them for entertainment. One day, he went out for business, and while his family was feeding the birds, one of Mr. Yang's favorite white-feathered parrots escaped from its cage. Mr. Yang was quite upset when he returned and found out, but he couldn't blame his family deeply and remained unhappy for several days. Later, Mr. Yang wrote a poem about the flying bird, saying, "I love birds and rejoice, flapping wings learning to escape Zen. The empty cage remains, exhaustion shows its return is known." The bird's heart overflows in his words.

Record of the Grand Gathering at Fudan University

— Shen Zhenchao

Fudan University held a grand gathering for its 25th anniversary for three days. Jiangwan Road was suddenly filled with traffic. There were ball games on the 16th, the anniversary ceremony, the awarding of honorary doctorates, and the opening of the girls' dormitory on the 17th, but I was unable to attend due to circumstances. On the 18th, my sister Hui came from Suzhou, so we went together. After lunch, we set off, but there was no room even to stand on the long-distance bus. When we arrived at Fudan, the carnival had not yet opened.

Few Tickets, Many People The carnival was held in the gymnasium, and upon entering, we saw only a mass of heads moving around. We couldn't sit or stand properly. Just as we were feeling frustrated, my friend Lu Chen came from outside. Lu is a student at Fudan and will graduate next summer. He is an excellent athlete and a pillar of Fudan's basketball team. Seeing the situation, he apologized for the inadequate reception and quickly found a ticket for us, leading us to a special seat. However, all the seats were taken, so he managed to find one in the front row. I then sat on a blank piece of paper covering a board next to it. The students of Fudan University treated us warmly, and I was deeply grateful.

Melodious Piano Music The curtain opened, and a female student, Ms. Ji Wanyi, performed a solo piano piece, creating an extremely gentle melody, clear and melodious like a nightingale singing in a valley. Her fingering skills were superb, but unfortunately, the order was not ideal, and those sitting in the back were unable to hear it fully. Ms. Ji graduated from Qiming Girls' School in Shanghai West and is beautiful and intelligent. Her beautiful piano playing has a long history.

Witty Dance Mr. Han Ligen performed a solo comic skit, wearing leather shoes and a long robe covered with a woman's half-sleeve jacket. First, he acted as an old country bumpkin visiting the Great Eastern Dance Hall, and then he spoke in various dialects, which were comical and made the whole hall roar with laughter. He said that people dance, but he dances at the Huangpu River, implying that those who are obsessed with dancing are in danger of ending up in the Huangpu River. His words were profound and meaningful, and his humor contained a solemn air.

Extremely Crowded and Embarrassing The special seats were limited, but there were many guests, making it difficult for the reception. Those who couldn't find seats had to stand, and even those who were sitting had to stand as well. Just as I was standing and watching, Ms. Ji Wanyi and her friend came from behind, saw the clean white paper on the board, and unknowingly sat down. Seeing this, I was extremely embarrassed but couldn't tell them directly. I was afraid of disturbing them by squeezing, but I couldn't avoid them. The Fudan students then asked the ladies to sit in the back, and I was able to sit down again. This also shows how crowded it was.

News of Sister Li Minghui I haven't heard from Ms. Li Minghui for a long time, and the information I have is contradictory. Suddenly, I heard someone behind me say that Li Minghui went to Hong Kong last week. If you want to get her address, you can ask at a bookstore on North Sichuan Road. Mr. Li is now in Harbin and will be returning to Shanghai soon. I knew that it was about Li Minghui, so I turned around and saw three or four of Mr. Li's students, including Ms. Zhang Meibao, telling a Fudan student.

Longing for the East Palace There were many other performances, including martial arts, Cantonese opera, and songs and dances, which I can't record in detail. The meeting ended when dusk was approaching. I met my friend Tao Lianghe, who is studying journalism. I asked him to guide me to see the whole school. Tao said that the East Palace (girls' dormitory) is not open today, which I heard with disappointment. Looking into the distance, I could only see the lights shining brightly and the female students chatting and laughing happily. Visiting the East Palace can only wait until next year. We smiled at each other and returned home.

Book Bed and Medicine Stove

— Meixi

Since entering the capital, it has been almost a month and a half. In my solitude, I am drunk and bedridden. There are poems by Ding Chang on my pillow, so I picked up some of his lines and got a few poems. Alas, Lan Cheng's words are less joyful, and Yu Xi's thoughts are more graceful. Even the sages of the past could not avoid sorrow when writing about current events, especially since the weather is cold with wind, and the days pass quickly. I hate being human and cannot be without emotion. There are precedents for fragrant crumbs and otter offerings. In this matter, this ambition is tears and sound. I will use my illness to let go of my worries. The poems say: "A hairpin and a pendant, I know the separation. The world is free to discuss, drunk half a glass. Rouse the sea plum red under the curtain, the spirit in my chest wants to become a cloud." "Autumn heart like the sea, like the tide. Dust becomes dust, feelings do not subside. Can I repay the three lives of hidden grievance, golden hair and sideburns floating in the wind." "The moonlit ground and cloud steps are specially allowed to be cold, and clear tears return in a dream. Now, after the great tribulation of rebirth, I will manage to see the mountains for fifty years." "A hundred years of heart will return to peace, experiencing the world of flowers and enlightenment. Do not complain that the ferry bridge is a guest for a long time, and the ends of the earth shake hands with all the literati (referring to Shou Juan, Cang Jun, and Yanhong)." "Red is lovesickness, green is sorrow. Over the years, flowers and plants have been cold in Suzhou. What can a scholar do with his strategy, abandon the mountains and lakes for a flute of autumn." "There are other words of weeping before the wine, what other method can send off this life. Plum souls and chrysanthemum shadows have been discussed, and if one day the hate sea is filled." "Clouds and smoke in ten thousand forms engulf the horse's hooves, singing and weeping endlessly, every word is true. It turns out that the peach blossom heart is not dead, and only allows the body to store the kernel of spring." "Double paddles and seagull waves, again and again. Do not allow red beans to dominate lovesickness. Fragrant orchids judge the past wrong, ashamed of drifting and not having a period." "Tired eyes by the zither overlook the wilderness, tears wet the red skirt and never end. Eliminate my mountain and snow complaints, a line of emerald ink, a sealed letter." "The unfinished end is still illusory, and the young man strikes his sword and blows the Xiao. The setting sun suddenly falls in the Central Plains, but there is only an autumn soul that cannot be summoned." "Looking north at Gu Ling, looking south at Wild Goose, do not betray the kindness of your parents for a hundred years. Do not stain your traveling clothes with ordinary tears, throw them into the flood and give them to the void." "Singing and crying, the predecessors are more sentimental, do not throw away your strength to trade talent. Light the broken wall with a lamp and burn poetry, and give it to the mandarin ducks to complain unevenly." (To be continued)

A Record of Art Studies in Rome (II)

— Wang Yachen

(1) The Ancient Colosseum This surviving ancient site is not only one of the largest existing buildings in the world, but also its ingenious arrangement of gates, the application of various Greek capitals, and its representation of the Tilus era. At that time, the arena could accommodate six thousand people. Historically, it was the site of the most brutal gladiatorial contests and was used as a killing field for clergy. When ancient Rome rejected foreign religions, countless Christians were sacrificed in the arena, devoured alive by wild beasts. There was also a cruel gladiatorial contest in which strong and healthy warriors competed in this arena. The winner would listen to the king's command, and the king would kill the loser by pointing his thumb down. If the king pointed up, the loser could live, but most losers were given death. There were often best friends who killed each other. The despotic king was extremely brutal. However, this arena remains today as the only symbol of ancient Rome.

(2) St. Peter's Basilica The scale of this church is even larger than St. Paul's. The outer square has more than three hundred large stone columns arranged in pairs. Each column can be embraced by three people. In the center of the square are two large fountains. Its solemnity and grandeur are unmatched. Upon entering the church, there are circular floor tiles of more than ten feet in length, which are the oldest objects. It is said that the church was rebuilt five hundred years ago. All the structures in the church were designed by the great Renaissance artist Wei Jia Zhu Gelang Jiluo. In the center of the upper part of the church are statues of the Virgin Mary and Jesus by Michelangelo at the age of twenty-five. On the right is a large iron door that is usually closed and opened on Sundays. Inside is a silver-gilt statue of the Virgin Mary, more than ten feet high. Next to the statue are two doors that lead directly to the Pope's residence, where the Roman Pope resides. This church measures one hundred and twenty-two meters in height from the ground to the top of the spire. In the center of the dome is a bronze pavilion made of three thousand four hundred tons of brass. Around the church are dozens of statues of popes from various eras, including the clergyman praying statue of the great sculptor Beruini, which expresses a very pious expression.

European Travel Correspondence (80)

— Liu Haisu

(3) Ten Days in Rome (3)

— The Immortal City La ville eternelle

June 1st Spanish Masterpieces Exhibition and Japanese Modern Painting Exhibition

Greco was a Spanish painter of the late 16th century whose reputation has only recently become widespread. Today, European art critics, whoever they may be, consider him to be the first giant of the Spanish school, or hold him in the same esteem as Velázquez. He was a radical pioneer. Velázquez's paintings were too stable, so many modern avant-garde artists especially revere Greco's paintings. He was born in Crete, Greece, in 1548 and died in Toledo, Spain, in 1614. At the age of twenty-five, he went to Venice and became a disciple of Titian, but he left and studied with Tintoretto, receiving a profound influence. Later, he studied the works of Michelangelo and Correggio in Rome. He was an extremely tragic painter and one of the most intensely mysterious in color. The human bodies he painted were slender, and the divine and holy figures in his religious paintings had a human sweetness. They were all tall and thin men with long chins and pointed toes. He loved to use dark green and blue, completely abandoning the flamboyant style of the Venetian school and changing it to a cold and solemn tone. His bold brushstrokes never adhered to detail, and the scenes were often filled with the excitement of deep depression and magic. His mad heroic posture and spiritual expression were a destruction of the great masters of Italy since Giotto and a progression. He was immersed in studying the Italian school and was able to break away from the conventions of the Italian school, using a sense of detachment to oppose the graceful style of the Florentine school. However, his mysterious tones were still transformed from the Venetian school. His deep tones express the pulse of ecstasy and fantasy and contain a strong expression of Eastern color, because his character was too unique, so there were no successors. However, he gave more vital force to modern art than Velázquez and Goya. Cézanne's deep color scales and solemn realistic style all owe to him. This is easy to see. Among the works I saw this time, the most pleasing are the following:

39 The Tears of St. Peter is not only a masterpiece of Greco but also the only representative work of the Spanish school. Especially in this subject, no one has painted it so violently and sharply, showing the trembling of the nerves. This is really a special stroke in the history of painting.

Financial Gold Market Rebounds from Low Point

The situation fluctuated unpredictably. Yesterday, the gold market rebounded from a low point, but only managed to hover around a certain level. After repeated advances and retreats, it ultimately showed signs of decline. The price fluctuated by one or two taels at a time. Overall, the market rose by four and a half taels. It is worth noting that the price had previously broken the 70-tael mark. The exchange rate also showed some signs of easing, with banks slightly selling off. Market sentiment was weak, almost in a state of bewilderment and loss. Trading among various firms was divergent, and arbitrage was very active. There was a lot of coming and going, with Wanxing Shunli, Yuancheng, Yongchun Yuan, Yongyuan, and others mainly buying, while Yuanmao, Yongyu, Dafuchang, and others were mainly selling. The Scale Market Indeed Fell

Market Overview

During the past week, foreign scales once fell and then rebounded. There was a definite possibility of a downward trend in sight. Subsequently, due to various reasons, it stood firm. Suddenly, the special reason for the sharp rise the day before yesterday was indeed difficult to be a benchmark. In fact, the actual foundation was ultimately weak, resulting in a downward trend yesterday. US Government Devotes Effort to Rescuing Cotton and Wheat

Over the past two years, the US government, with the Department of Agriculture and the Federal Farm Board as agencies, has continued rural relief efforts. For this purpose, with the agreement of Congress, a huge amount of 500 million yuan has been spent. Recently, it is planned to request an additional expenditure of 500 million yuan. The government devotes the main force of relief to the wheat and cotton markets. The relief policies implemented so far can be divided into three items: (1) Improvement of sales organization: The government first pays attention to this, improving the efficiency of the sales organization taken out by American farmers from the past, and vigorously promoting the organization of broader joint combinations. (2) Government purchase: Because the federal government buys spot goods in the market, the government owns a very large inventory of wheat and cotton. (3) Reduction of cultivated acreage: The government uses all propaganda to persuade farmers to reduce the cultivated acreage of wheat, prevent wheat production above domestic consumption, and has no intention of competing with Australian, Canadian, and Argentine wheat in the overseas market. Because of the government's strength, the adverse effects of falling prices of wheat, cotton, etc. under the above three major policies have been greatly eased. The opposition said that the government's share issue ultimately ended in a major failure. It can be proved by the current low prices of agricultural products. On the one hand, the Federal Farm Board's assistance to the joint combination organization of American farmers in states such as Alganklons, Lucy, Ainai, and California has been visible. It is planned that after the joint combination of farmers in each state is established, a central rice farmers' association will be jointly organized to recruit powerful farmers to cooperate with the Federal Farm Board to assist farmers throughout the United States.

The Milan market's Italian cocoon market remains sluggish. Yuanzhi Tribute Cloth is Becoming Increasingly Popular

Since the autumn, sales of Yuanqing straight tribute cloth have increased sharply, and the sales price has also risen significantly. After the sharp contraction in foreign exchange, few merchants have placed orders, resulting in a shortage of arrivals. The stocks stored in various Shanghai warehouses are gradually being sold out, with supply falling short of demand. In recent days, demand from both local and foreign buyers has been strong, and retail sales have already increased significantly. The previously allocated tribute cloth is now sold out, so further purchases must be made. Yesterday, the trend at the association was brisk, and sales prices for general goods increased by 1-2 qian. Other ordinary Yuanzhi tribute cloth, such as three-tael-plus and four-tael-three-four-qian grades, are temporarily difficult to select. The market sentiment for straight tribute cloth is particularly brisk, and demand from the Harbin gang is very strong. It is reported that 40-50 boxes were sold last week, with prices changing three times a day, and the shortage and briskness are even greater than that of double-sided high-quality goods.

Automobile News

Special Articles

New York Automobile Traffic

— Pei Gan

New York's traffic is world-renowned. According to actual time studies, the average speed of cars and horses on the north-south streets south of 42nd Street is 11.3 miles per hour. Under these conditions, the aforementioned streets see over 10,000 vehicles pass per hour. The congestion on the streets is really due to the island shape of New York City, which is 12.5 miles long and 2.5 miles wide. Near the pointed top, the widest point is only 1.5 miles. In this small area, countless millions of automobiles and carriages pass through every day. The automobile routes between New York and Manhattan are connected by large bridges. In addition to some large bridges, there are also more than 20 waterways, with hundreds of harbor ferries coming and going every day, carrying passengers and transporting vehicles. As for the Dutch tunnel connecting New York and New Jersey, it is another shortcut for traffic in both places.

Although New York's vehicles are so congested, the convenience of its vehicle traffic is truly astonishing. The police order the continuous flow of vehicles very quickly. From Battery Park to Fort Henry Road, the automatic opening and closing of red stop and green go vehicle traffic lights can be seen everywhere. Delays and accidents in the traffic on various streets are not commonly seen. The Times Square area in the heart of New York's theater district is the most difficult place in the world for vehicles to move through. It is only 12 blocks long and 5 blocks wide, and every night, the total number of people going to theaters and other entertainment venues is over half a million. A dance hall in a certain hotel there can hold 7,500 people. Madison Square Garden can hold over 25,000 people during major sports competitions. 96 major entertainment venues have audiences entering and exiting at the same time within the same 20 to 30 minutes every night. Recently, in order to solve this difficult situation, in these areas, parking is prohibited from 7:45 AM to 9:00 AM and from 10:30 PM onwards. In addition, rules for left and right turns at intersections have been established, and pedestrian rules have been set. Since the implementation of these measures, the speed and safety of traffic have increased by 30 percent.

The most difficult aspect of New York traffic is the handling of direct traffic. Manhattan Island itself is very narrow, and the usual traffic flow is already extremely congested. In addition to this, there are thousands of sightseeing vehicles passing through. A bridge building plan was created for this purpose. People from the south and west can take the northeastern route or bypass the area altogether, thus avoiding the hassle of going through Manhattan. Automobile drivers can avoid the congestion and delays of New York streets. This plan is nothing short of a blessing for travelers. But this statement is just a plan. If it is to be implemented, the current situation must be completely reformed. The current branch roads are expanded to accommodate outside vehicles. The current flat roads are dedicated to the special use of free-flowing vehicles. A two-story flat road, as wide as a sidewalk, is for pedestrians to walk on. The ground floor of large stores is used as a receiving area, and the floor is moved to the upper floor. Another suggestion for a new plane is to create an elevated avenue along the edge of Manhattan Island, from the Queensboro Bridge, east to 59th Street, and west to 72nd Street. New York's declaration of war on congested traffic began with the elevated avenue on Park Avenue at 40th Street, extending to Grand Central Terminal and through the new buildings of New York Central New House.

For ten years, the tall copper tower on Fifth Avenue, which used to display red and green lights to direct vehicle traffic, is now being demolished due to the needs of the times. The area where it stood has now been cleared and left with much empty space. As for the traffic lights on the tower, they have been moved to the roadside pillars to continue their work. The third step in solving traffic difficulties is the construction of a 21,300-foot elevated avenue located west of the Hudson River between Canal Street and 72nd Street. Once this road is completed, it can relieve the direct traffic of the north-south avenue. Its completion is expected in 1932. This elevated avenue has two 30-foot wide roads, which can accommodate 5,000 to 9,000 cars per hour. Its speed can be 35 miles per hour. The height is about 14 to 18 feet above the ground. This road can also be raised and lowered at intersections with important roads.

How to Accept a New Car

— Ding Zuzhe

Matters to Note

When a new car is shipped from the factory, the radiator and fuel tank are usually drained. In some cases, the machine oil in the oil pan is also removed. After receiving the car, check these three places and replenish any that are empty.

Before a new car leaves the factory, the factory personnel will install all the necessary items. However, during transportation by boat and car, loss or damage is inevitable. The recipient must not be careless and must inspect the car carefully.

Sometimes, there are also new cars delivered to the buyer with sufficient gasoline, machine oil, and water, and all parts complete. The buyer should also carefully inspect the car, because it often happens that a car is driven from the car dealership by its employee to the buyer's residence without any difficulty, but if the buyer does not check the car upon receipt, the purchased car suddenly develops problems upon delivery. This happens often, and it is too late to regret it afterwards.

The inspection procedure can be done according to the instruction manual of the purchased car. The manual lists all the included repair tools, which should be checked once to prevent any shortages. Car dealership workers often take one or two of these small tools for themselves because they are easy to carry. Buyers often do not pursue the matter because the value of these tools is not high, but they realize the importance of these small tools when they need them. The exterior of the new car should be checked for any damage, and whether the spare tire, spare wheel, or spare ring are available. Check that each light is intact and whether it can light up. In short, no small parts should be missing. What is especially important is to check whether the car brand, model, and engine number listed on the car sales contract signed by the car dealership are completely consistent with the vehicle received, in order to prevent being cheated.

If the new car received is disassembled from a wooden box, in addition to assembling each part, you should pay attention to the following points:

Tires: Each tire should be complete and undamaged and have enough air pressure. The spare tire should also be inflated before being hung on the car.

Water, Gasoline, Machine Oil: Fill the radiator with clean water. After the engine has warmed up, add a little machine oil. Fill the fuel tank with gasoline. If any overnight sediment is found, it must be drained first. Transmission parts: Check whether the machine oil stored in the transmission and rear axle housing is full. The oil plug heads in these two places can be removed. If the oil level has dropped below the position of the oil plug head, add a little machine oil until oil overflows from the hole (at the plug head).

Transmission Method of Gears Engaging Simultaneously

— Ji Ren

Among the many improvements of the 1931 overhead valve New Buick, the newest and most noticeable to car owners and drivers is the transmission method of gears engaging simultaneously. According to Mr. Chris (manager of the Shanghai General Motors Company), this type of transmission is only available on the most expensive cars manufactured by the American General Motors Manufacturing Plant. The smoothness and fluency of its mechanical power flow is only available in this eight-cylinder engine car. All new Buick cars (except the 8-50 model) have this feature.

Buick's transmission method of gears engaging simultaneously allows the first gear to be shifted to second gear and then to third gear at any speed, and reverse gear can be engaged at the same time without any conflict or obstruction. There are countless benefits, and the absence of grinding noise during operation further enhances the joy of driving.

The transmission with gears engaging simultaneously ensures safe driving. Drivers know that it is safer to use second gear when going down steep slopes to prevent the speed from becoming too fast and to avoid accidents. Often the height of the mountain slopes is difficult to guess. The degree of slope is not known until the actual descent. Therefore, it is most difficult to engage gears when the speed is high. A transmission with gears engaging simultaneously is essential to deal with the difficulties at that time.

No matter how high the car speed is, the transmission with gears engaging simultaneously can immediately return from no gear to second gear without hesitation. When in use, the driver only needs to depress the transmission pedal and push the gear lever to its original position, and the car will be easy to use. Moreover, engaging gears before departure is completely automatic and very stable, which can extend the life of the internal mechanical parts of the car.

The movement of the transmission with gears engaging simultaneously is extremely smooth. It can be controlled freely on various road surfaces without fear of clumsy shaking, and the speed can be increased from low to high immediately.

Page 20

Speed and passengers can be unaware.

The manufacturing of this device is exquisite and the usage is simple, not a false assumption, and not a temporary secret. This mechanism is purely mechanical and scientific, requires no adjustment, and automatically regulates.

The principle of the transmission with gears engaging simultaneously is quite ingenious. Briefly, when the first gear is shifted to second gear and then to third gear, or when reverse gear is engaged, there are two rotating wheels that transmit at the same time, and the speed is equal to avoid conflict. Although ordinary transmissions also have two gears, they do not transmit at the same time. The rotation of one gear is often equal to the engine speed, and the rotation of the other gear is often the same as the car speed. During shifting, the car or engine speed must first be equal to the accelerator or brake before the gear can be engaged without bumping. From this point of view, it is really difficult for ordinary transmissions to change gears in time when driving on rough roads.

The gear transmits mechanical power to the gear lever on the sliding surface of the main shaft. When the gear shaft rotates, it first touches the power transmission box of the pointed cylinder and meshes tightly with the teeth of the toothed power transmission box and the rotating gear, so that the free-rotating gear has a direct relationship with the gear lever. The center of the transmission with gears engaging simultaneously is a simple pointed cylinder power transmission box that grips the rotating gear tightly and accurately. The speed of the two rotating gears. This mechanical device is extremely accurate. After the pointed cylinder power transmission box aligns the speed, the toothed power transmission box and the rotating gear follow. Working in the pointed cylinder power transmission box, after the two gears are completely merged, the pointed cylinder power transmission box automatically disengages.

There is no change in how to use the gears. Now, when the driver pushes the gears, he feels light, nimble, and responsive, and allows the pointed cylinder power transmission box to complete its speed matching work before the toothed power transmission box makes contact. Therefore, the previous clumsy method of engaging gears and the worry about increasing and decreasing speed can be avoided.

Translated Compilation

Car News from Across the Sea

— Tan Zidian

Tessatur Test Drive: The new 27-horsepower Tessatur 8 car recently had a test drive on Mount Sule in Australia. The car carried a total of 14 people, weighing 1.75 tons. It climbed the mountain at full speed, and the body and engine of the car were not damaged at all, and it could travel an average of 24 miles per hour, which is not easy.

Chrysler Wins in Mexico: Recently, in a race in Mexico City, Chrysler won all three A, B, and C class championships, winning supreme honors. In Class A, the 75-mile winding mountain road was won by the Chrysler 77 sports car, taking only one hour, nine minutes, and twenty-one seconds, surpassing the previous record by three and two-fifths seconds. Class B was won by the Chrysler 66, with the same route as Class A, taking one hour, sixteen minutes, and fifty-one seconds. Class C was also won by the Chrysler 66, taking one hour, twenty-two minutes, and fifty-three seconds.

Gas Tax in New South Wales: According to a report from the Australian Road Authority, the state of New South Wales collected a total of 1,390,458 pounds in gas taxes and 408,665 pounds in registration fees by the end of June of this year. The following is a record of cars in the area for the last three years:

Gas Tax Registration Fee

1928 1,110,280 pounds 139,198 pounds

1929 1,310,56 pounds 365,309 pounds

1930 1,390,458 pounds 408,66 pounds

30,000 Public Cars in Victoria: In order to promote education, the Victorian Department of Education has ordered 30,000 public cars from the United States specifically for transporting students to and from various schools.

Opening of the International Automobile Exhibition

Reuters, London, 16th – The 1930 International Automobile Exhibition opened today at Olympia. The variety and quality of the displays are unprecedented. Old-style automobiles from 1896 to 1913 are also on display. The new cars have lower bodies, better brakes, and sturdier construction, while prices are lower. The four-cylinder car seems to have been overshadowed by the six-cylinder car. Half of the cars on display are six-cylinder. However, a certain factory in Coventry still displays four-cylinder cars because they are more economical. There are over seventy participating factories. The United States, France, Italy, Belgium, and Germany all have products on display. British manufacturers' styles and workmanship are considered the best among family cars on display.

Shanghai Market

Market News

The Liji Pharmacy on Qipan Street announces that their establishment was founded in Guangdong during the Guangxu era and has been around for several decades. The various efficacious plasters, pills, powders, and granules they produce are made with authentic ingredients and refined craftsmanship, remaining unchanged for a long time. They have been sold in Guangdong and the Nanyang Islands, enjoying a great reputation and widespread praise. This year, a branch was established and operated at the Qingyunli entrance on North Sichuan Road in Shanghai, and it has been quite prosperous. Recently, due to insufficient space for development at that location, they have moved to the south end of Jiaotong Road on Qipan Street, where they continue to operate as usual. Since the opening, all self-made medicines sold have been offered on a buy-one-get-one-free basis, resulting in brisk business. The best-selling medicines are Cough Remedy, Tai Huo Luo Dan, Life-Saving Pill, Gynecology White Phoenix Pill, Ginseng and Velvet Health Pill, and Universal Relief Pill, and it is said that demand greatly exceeds supply.
